 unhone bhi gambheer ke saath milakar pari ko dhire-dhire aage badhaayaa

 unhone 60 gendon kaa saamana karte hue 31 ran banaae
 Lasith Malinga bowled him clean and showed the way to the pavilion
 dhoni kaa sthaan lene aae rohit sharma ek baar phir flop sabit hue

 vah apana khaataa bhi nahin khol sake

 do overon ke baad shatakaveer gambheer bhi pavilion lautne ko majaboor ho gaye

 But Suresh Raina and Irfan Pathan achieved this goal on their own and led the Indian team to victory
 raina ne 45 gendon par chah chaukon or ek chakke kii madad se 65 ran banaae jabaki pathan ne 31 gendon par 34 ran banaae
 11 for the fifth wicket between the two
 1 overon main 92 ranon kii saajhedaari hui
 Earlier, Sri Lanka won the toss and scored 286 runs for the loss of six wickets in the allotted 50 overs
 shuruaati jhatkon ke baad srilanka kii pari ladkadaa gai thi
 He had lost the wickets of the top three batsmen on a total of just 20 but after that Mahela Jayawardene and Kumar Sangakkara pulled the Sri Lankan team out of trouble
 antim overon main angelo maithyuj or jivan mendis ne shatkeey saajhedaari kar team ko majboot sthiti main pahunchaa diya
 Sri Lanka won the toss and decided to bat first
 kul yoga main abhi nau ran hi jude the ki tillakaratne dilashaan ko chaar ran ke nijee yoga par jahir khan ne bold kar pavilion bhej diya
 Upul Tharanga also went for a total of 19 in the fifth over
 vah aath ran hi bana sake
 On the ball of Zaheer, captain Mahendra Singh Dhoni caught his catch behind the wicket
 tisare nambar par ballebaaji karne aae dinesh chandimal to apana khaataa bhi nahin khol sake
 Irfan Pathan lbw to him
 iske baad sangakaara or jayavardhane ne chauthe wicket ke liye 121 ranon kii saajhedaari kar apni team ko mushkil paristhitiyon se baahar nikaala
 Sri Lanka suffered a fourth setback in the 30th over as Jayawardene
 jayavardhane ne 65 ranon kii shandaar pari kheli
 During this, he faced 79 balls and hit five fours
 rahul sharma kii gend par vah pagabaadha out hue
 Mathews, who came to replace Jayawardene, played with Sangakkara
 donon ke bich paanchaven wicket ke liye 41 ranon kii saajhedaari hui
 Sangakkara continued to run at a total of 182
 unhone 95 gendon kaa saamana kiya or 73 ran banaae
 During this, he hit five fours
 us samay tak lag rahaa tha ki srilanka kii team 250 ke aankade ko paar nahin kar paaegi lekin maithyuj ne mendis ke saath milakar na sirf pari ko aage badhaayaa balki uske baad bina koi wicket ganvaae team kaa score 286 tak pahunchaa diya
 Mathews hit a quick innings of 71 off 57 balls
 is dauraan unhone paanch chauke or ek chakka lagaaya
 Mendis scored 45 off 40 balls and hit three fours and a six
 donon ne chathe wicket ke liye 104 ranon kii naabad saajhedaari kii
 Zaheer Khan was the most successful bowler for India
 unhone do wicket hasil kiye
 Pathan, Ashok Dinda and Sharma got one wicket each
 dinda bahut kharchile sabit hue
 In his 10-over quota, he scored 76 runs
 tippaniyan The Indian team has now taken a 2–1 lead in the series
 is match ke liye srilankai team main ek parivartan kiya gaya tha
 Jeevan Mendis replaced batsman Lahiru Thirimanne in Sri Lanka's last XI team
 bhartiya team ne is mukaable ke liye apni team main do badlaav kiye the
 Leg-spinner Rahul Sharma and fast bowler Ashok Dinda were replaced in the playing XI, replacing Pragyan Ojha and Umesh Yadav
 iske baad captain mahendra singh dhoni ne khud maidan par morcha sambhaala
 He, along with Gambhir, moved the innings slowly forward
 lekin 36wein over kii pehali gend par dhoni bhi apana wicket ganvaa baithe
 He scored 31 runs, facing 60 balls
 lasith malinga ne unhen clin bold kar pavilion kii raah dikhaai
 Rohit Sharma who came to replace Dhoni proved to be a flop once again
 malinga kii pehali hi gend par vah chakma kha gaye or pagabaadha qaraar die gaye
 He could not even open his account
 malinga ne lagaataar do gendon par do wicket lekar bhartiya team ko ek baar phir baikfoot par dhakel diya
 After two overs, century Gambhir was also forced to return to the pavilion
 vah ran out hue
 Gambhir scored 102 off 101 balls
 unhone 10 chauke lagaae
 After Gambhir's dismissal, it was felt that it would be difficult for the Indian team to return to this match

 lekin suresh raina or irfan pathan ne apane dam par is lakshya ko hasil kiya or bhartiya team ko jeet dilaai
 Raina scored 65 runs off 45 balls with the help of six fours and a six while Pathan scored 34 off 31 balls
 donon ke bich paanchaven wicket par 11
 There was a 92-run partnership in 1 over
 isse pehle srilanka ne toss jitkar pehle ballebaaji karte hue nirdhaarit 50 overon main chah wicket ke nuksaan par 286 ran banaae
 Sri Lanka's innings faltered after the initial setbacks
 usne mahaj 20 ke yoga par chotii ke teen ballebaajon ke wicket ganvaa die the lekin iske baad mahela jayavardhane or kumaar sangakaara ne milakar srilankai team ko mushkilon se nikaala
 Angelo Mathews and Jeevan Mendis scored a century partnership in the final overs to bring the team to a strong position
 srilanka ne toss jitkar pehle ballebaaji kaa faisla kiya tha
 Only nine runs were added to the total that Tilakaratne Dilshan was bowled by Zaheer Khan on a personal total of four runs and sent to the pavilion
 paanchaven over main 19 ke kul yoga par upul tharanga bhi chal die
 He could only score eight runs
 jahir kii gend par captain mahendra singh dhoni ne wicket ke peeche unka kaich lapka
 Dinesh Chandimal, who came to bat on the third number, could not even open his account
 irfan pathan ne unhen pagabaadha out kiya
 After this, Sangakkara and Jayawardene shared 121 runs for the fourth wicket to take their team out of difficult situations

 Renowned sitar pundit Ravi Shankar has died in a hospital in San Diego
 vah 92 saal ke the or pichley kuch samay se biimaar chal rahe the
 He was operated on 7 December
 unhen 1999 main bharat ratna se sammanit kiya gaya tha
 Born in a Bengali Brahmin family on April 7, 1920 in Varanasi, Pandit Ravi Shankar grew up in a musical environment since childhood and was interested in musical instruments
 ravishankar apane bade bhai udaishankar ke baile trup main the
 Pandit Ravi Shankar was honored with many great accolades of the country and the world
 inhen mashhoor antarrashtriya sammaan grami aword bhi mila tha
 Apart from this, he was also awarded the Magsaysay Award
 pandit ravishankar 1986 se 1992 tak rajyasabha ke sadsy bhi rahe
 Pandit Ravi Shankar learned sitar from Ustad Alauddin Khan, whom he fondly called Baba
 unhone 'dharti ke laal' or 'nicha nagar' jaisi filmon main sangeet bhi diya
 Mohammad Iqbal's' Saare Jahan Se Achchha
 
 
 ' kii dhun bhi pandit ravishankar kii banaai hui he
 The year 1966 was extremely important for Pandit Ravi Shankar, as the same year George Harrison, a member of the famous music group 'beatles', became his disciple
 iske baad pandit ravishankar antarrashtriya str par behad vikhyath ho gaye
 The international music world has been mourned by the death of Pandit Ravi Shankar and music lovers from all over the world are paying tribute to him
 kuch din purv hi pandit ravishankar ne bollywood abhinayta atimabh bachchan se baat karne ke liye unhen phone kiya tha
 Pandit Ravi Shankar was admitted to the Skips Memorial Hospital in La Jolla last Thursday after complaining of breathlessness

 ab jabaki pulavama atake ke baad paak kaa aatanki cheharaa phir duniya ke saamne aayaa he, paak adhikrut kashmir ne UNHRC main kaha he ki pakistani sena bharat ke khilaaf proxi waar main aatankiyon kaa istemaal karti he

 unhone kaha, 'pakistani sena ab kashmiriyon se halke hathiyaaron ke bajaay aatmghaatee hamalon ke aadesh de rahi he

 'pok human rights activist and second speaker of the panel, Missfer Hassan, said that there has been a counter-attack for the last 71 years
 unhone kaha ki haal ke pulavama atake ne do parmaanu sampann takaton ko yuddh ke muhane par laakar khadaa kar diya he

 pakistan kii khufia agency iesai bharat main ghuspaith karaane ke liye lagaataar seemaa ke us paar se koshish kar rahaa he khufia report se kis baat kaa us samay khulaasa hua tha ki april main barf pighalane ke saath hi lonching pad main aatankiyon kii sankhya zyada dekhi gai thi
 Recently, a report sent to the Ministry of Home Affairs by the Multi Agency Center has revealed that till May, terrorists have infiltrated from across the border about 115 times
 pakistan kii taraf se is saal ab tak 115 baar aatanki ghuspaith kii koshish kii gai
 In which the attempt to infiltrate 19 terrorists was successful, in the remaining infiltration, the terrorists were either killed or the terrorists could not enter India
 aapako bataa den ki kashmir ke andar jis tareeke se suraksha agenciyaan is samay line of control or international border par chaukasee barat rahi he
 In this way, the terrorists, who are unable to make infiltration at this time, are either being piled up near the border or the operation of killing all those who enter inside the border is going on continuously through the security forces
 
 khufia reportse is baat kaa khulaasa hua he ki aatanki kashmir ghati main jitani sankhya main maujuud he
 Its district-wise report has also been made in which according to information 258 terrorists have been identified in 13 districts, in which the number of local terrorists is more, the number of fellow infiltrators is less
 sutara bataate hai ki kashmir ghati main is samay kareeb 130 local aatankwaadi maujuud hai, or 128 videshi aatanki jisamen lashkar ke aatanki sabase zyada hai
 According to the information, the security agencies have been continuously overwhelmed by the manner in which the terrorists have been operating in the last few days
 isi se desparat hokar aatankiyon ne somvaar ko amarnath yatra main suraksha ke liye lagaae gaye jammu-kashmir police party par bhi hamalaa kiya uske baad aatanki vahaan se batch nikle
 According to CRPF sources, strict security arrangements have been made for the Amarnath Yatra this year, all passengers, whether they are going from Baltal area or via Pahalgam, are being provided full security to their convoys through security forces
